Truth Revealed About the Murder of Chen Hongfu: Roadside Rumors Proven Accurate; Children Tell of Father's Murder; Two Children Suddenly Hidden and Unavailable for Court Summons

Chen Hongfu, a farmer from Yanjiacao, Gaoqiao, Pudong, of Chongming origin, was murdered one night last month. After the case was reported, the local court prosecutor detained and arrested the victim’s wife, Chen Wangshi, and the victim’s maternal uncle, Lu Zhiliang, as suspects. It is now known that since the case occurred, people in the area have been talking about it, saying that Lu Zhiliang (also from Chongming) was a foreman coppersmith at the public concession's electric company, earning a good monthly income, and had dozens of acres of farmland in Yanjiacao, Gaoqiao. Previously, in 1931, his nephew Chen Hongfu rented eight acres of land from his maternal uncle Lu Zhiliang to cultivate. Unexpectedly, since renting, it has been four years and the rent had not been paid. Lu repeatedly demanded payment without success. This spring, Lu Zhiliang and his wife, Li, gathered several people and went to Chen Hongfu's house to forcibly remove glutinous rice. Chen refused and reported the matter to the police, who detained Lu and Li and sent them to the court prosecutor's office for questioning and detention, resulting in a decision not to prosecute. Chen Hongfu refused to accept this and filed an appeal to the High Court. Lu Zhiliang resented his nephew Chen Hongfu for resorting to such rogue tactics and hated him deeply. It was discovered that after Chen Hongfu was murdered, according to Chen's thirteen-year-old daughter, "My father was indeed beaten to death by my maternal uncle (referring to Lu Zhiliang) along with three young men whom I didn’t know. My maternal uncle choked my father with his hands, my mother held down his feet, and the three young men beat him with benches, killing him." (According to the court's examination, Chen Hongfu's left and right ribs were broken.) "Then they dragged my father's body out to cover up their crime." The girl recounted everything she witnessed regarding her father's murder to her neighbors Zhang Qinglang and Yang the Blind, etc. Zhang and the others were greatly astonished to hear this, and everyone in the neighborhood was shocked. After learning about these facts, the court ordered Zhang Qinglang, Yang the Blind, and the local headman Gao Linquan to appear in court the day before yesterday for a lengthy investigation. As a result, they were told to leave and await further instructions. However, the one son and one daughter of the deceased, being young and ignorant of the consequences, spoke of their father's murder to everyone they met. Recently, someone hid the two children, so the court repeatedly summoned them without success. There are probably clues to this. After the incident, the local police station summoned the victim’s wife, Chen Wangshi, who claimed that her husband was beaten to death for stealing taro from someone else's field. The police station indeed found half a sack of taro in her house. However, the investigation proved that the taro came from Chen Hongfu's own field and was not stolen. It is evident that Chen Wangshi's statement was flawed. It is believed that once the court conducts a thorough investigation into this shocking murder case, carefully uncovering the truth, the truth will come to light and the injustice will be redressed. It was discovered that the appeal Chen Hongfu filed with the High Court was rejected. The court was delivering the notice at the time Chen Hongfu's body was lying in the field and the judge was conducting the inspection.

Jianghai Customs Orders Prohibition of Manufacturing Manual Cigarette Rolling Tools

Announcement Issued Yesterday to Notify Merchants

The Jianghai Customs issued Announcement No. 1490 yesterday, stating that it has received an order to prohibit the manufacture, sale, or purchase of manual cigarette rolling tools. The announcement stated, "We are now under orders from the Ministry of Finance that all tools used for rolling manual cigarettes shall be prohibited from manufacture, sale, and purchase. Anyone violating this regulation shall have their machinery confiscated and destroyed, and shall also be fined up to ten times the value. Upon receiving this order, we must comply with it. We hereby announce this to all merchants." Signed, Supervisor Tang Haian, Tax Commissioner Ba Runsen.

Public Bus Fares Revised by the Public Works Department

The British-owned China General Omnibus Company submitted a request to the Public Works Department of the Public Concession on October 23 to revise fares. After consideration by the Bureau, there were many unclear points regarding the new prices proposed by the company. The company was then ordered to provide detailed reasons for the revision of fares for each route and section, awaiting consideration. Subsequently, the company stated in a letter that the company was suffering great losses under the current fares. Therefore, the purpose of re-pricing was to increase operating income. The company had recently spent more than 500,000 yuan on the purchase of double-decker buses. In terms of comfort and convenience, the low prices were only found in a few countries in the world. Even with long-distance fares, the fare per mile was only 2 fen and 1 hao and 4 li of a dollar. Recently, the company also felt that the previously set prices were often unbalanced, so it had to be revised to develop the business. Subsequently, after negotiations between the head of the finance department of the Public Works Department and representatives of the company, the original prices were slightly modified. The pricing in some places was indeed lower than the current prices. The revised prices have been approved by the board of directors of the Public Works Department and will take effect on January 1 of the following year.

Notice for Owners of Private Hand-Pulled Rickshaws to Renew Licenses

All owners of private hand-pulled rickshaws in the Public Concession who wish to continue to obtain a license for 1936 must obtain it before January 20 at the Private Hand-Pulled Rickshaw Licensing Office at 596 Gongping Road. Those who go after the deadline will be given a new license plate number and charged a registration fee of 5 jiao in addition to the license fee. The application form is issued by the Public Works Department. Rickshaw owners can obtain it from the Licensing Office on Gongping Road, the Public Works Department's Tax Office, or the nearest police station. After filling out the application form, submit it along with the current quarterly license fee of 8 dollars to the Licensing Office. To avoid delays, owners of rickshaws who are renewing their licenses should pay attention to ensuring that all the details written on the application form are correct, and that all seals, signatures, etc., match the previous quarter. Furthermore, owners of private hand-pulled rickshaws should note that they should properly keep their license plates. After the license fee is stopped, it should be returned to the Licensing Office, the Public Works Department's Tax Office, or the nearest police station. Otherwise, the license fee will continue to be borne by them until the license plate is returned. The office hours of the Licensing Office on Gongping Road are stated below: From January 3 to January 20 (inclusive): 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM, 1:30 PM to 4:00 PM. From January 21 to March 31 (inclusive): 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM, 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM. On Saturdays, the office closes at 11:30 AM.

Municipal Council Seriously Cracks Down on Public Buses Emitting Black Smoke

The Municipal Council's strict crackdown on public buses emitting black smoke along the road has been reported in the newspapers several times before. According to news from the Municipal Council, the Public Works Department has conducted an investigation into the matter and has prepared a report for submission to the board of directors for review. According to the report, the China General Omnibus Company has made considerable efforts in terms of manpower and financial resources to find ways to reduce black smoke, and there has been significant improvement in fact. Furthermore, it is now the middle of winter, and the evaporation of gasoline is also more difficult, and January and February are the coldest months of the year. The inspectorate is using January and February as the standard for inspection to see how the improvement results, and then decide what to do. According to the department head's opinion, the Bureau need not take any further steps for the time being. It is reported that the above suggestion has been approved by the board of directors of the Municipal Council.

New Discovery in the Pigment Industry:

Monastral Fast Blue

British dye chemists have recently invented Monastral Fast Blue. After research by chemists from various countries, it is believed that this blue color has wider uses and more significant effects than egg blue and Prussian blue. The color is bright and vibrant, and it not only does not undergo any changes when exposed to light and heat, but it also has no chemical reaction to acids and sodas. It can be applied to the manufacture of soap, sealing wax, bills, oilcloth, cotton cloth, and cement, etc., making it a great discovery in the pigment industry in the last hundred years, and a great contribution to the modern scientific, artistic, and industrial worlds.

Prostitution Syndicate Boss Lu Laoqi Case Concluded

Sentencing Set for 31st Morning; Lu Bailed Out Yesterday by Yongfengtai

Lu Laoqi, a woman from Nanxiang also known as Wenying, age 35, formerly operated a brothel named Hanzhuang at 114 Chu Chia Chiao (now Avenue Hoche) in the French Concession, and currently resides at 55 Hu Chia Ko in the western suburbs of Shanghai. She was previously wanted for the private establishment of an illegal gambling syndicate and for suspicion of instigating the murder of Shao Wenbin (alias "A'liu" the groom) on the night of July 28, 1933. She was apprehended by French police on the 5th of this month and sent to the Second Special Court for investigation. After a thorough investigation by the police, there was deemed to be insufficient evidence to charge her with the murder. She was only publicly indicted by the prosecutor for gambling under Article 268 of the Criminal Code, based on reliable testimony from past offenders involved in the gambling syndicate. Lu also confessed that Xiao Pengtou, a guest, opened a flower gambling listening post in the Chinese area and invited her to invest, but that she did not set up a large syndicate. The police also sent detectives to search her brothel, but she immediately refused to participate. As for the murder, Lu firmly denied it and hired lawyers Jiang Yiping and Ma Shouhua to defend her. The court ordered that she be detained and that the hearing be rescheduled. Yesterday morning at around 10:00 AM, Wang Gangxu, the presiding judge of the criminal court of the Second Special Court, resumed the hearing of the case in the first criminal court. Lu's testimony was the same as the previous two times, but she claimed not to recognize any of the gamblers who had been arrested and punished. Then, Fei Xizhen, the police lawyer, and the defendant's defense lawyers cross-examined each other. After that, the court declared the hearing closed and scheduled the sentencing for the morning of the 31st of this month. The defendant Lu Wenying was to be released on a 6,000 yuan bail, and if no bail was posted, she would be remanded in custody. Subsequently, her family pleaded with Xie Tingxin, the owner of the Yongfengtai South Goods Store in Dongxinqiao Caishi Street, who was a fellow villager, to submit a written guarantee. Out of caution, the court summoned the guarantor Xie Tingxin to court and questioned him at 4:00 PM. Judge Wang opened the hearing, and Xie stated that he had been running the Yongfengtai South Goods Store for 11 years with a capital of 20,000 yuan. Although the market is now sluggish, his store has been open for a long time and can be maintained. He is a neighbor and fellow villager of Lu Wenying, has known her since childhood, and knows her to be honest, so he dared to guarantee that she would not flee. The judge told Xie that he must guarantee that the defendant would be available for all three trials and that he would be responsible for the 6,000 yuan guarantee. If the court ordered him to pay the guarantee, he must pay the 6,000 yuan in full without delay. If the defendant were to flee, he should immediately hand her over to the court, otherwise he would be held accountable for facilitating her escape, etc. Xie hesitated for a long time before fully agreeing and adding text and sealing the guarantee. The judge then ordered Lu Wenying to be taken away by her guarantor Xie Tingxin. Lu Laoqi, who had been in custody for three weeks, was now free.

Fishing Boats Transporting Fish to Shanghai Robbed En Route

Fish Cargo Completely Looted, Boatmen Wounded by Bandits

According to travelers arriving in Shanghai from Dinghai yesterday, a fishing boat robbery occurred in Shenjiamen, and fishermen were injured. The fishermen have petitioned the authorities for prompt protection. The detailed situation is as follows:

Fishing Boat Reaches Zhoushan. Recently, as the end of the year approaches, the market price of ribbonfish in Shanghai has shown a slight increase. Fishermen from Ningbo sent a large fishing boat to the Siheng Islands to collect fresh fish, obtaining more than sixty dan of ribbonfish, preparing to transport them to Shanghai. On the way back, due to the strong northwest wind, it was already late at night. The boat passed through Daotou in Shenjiamen, Zhoushan, where the fishermen and boatmen fell asleep. Unexpectedly, pirates arrived and took the opportunity to rob.

Robbery at Qingyantou. The fishing boat was towed to the Qingyantou waters by the pirate ship and docked beside the pirate ship. The bandits jumped aboard, wielding weapons, and threatened the fishermen. The four boatmen were guarded by the pirates and unable to resist, forced to comply with their demands. All sixty dan of ribbonfish in the boat were looted, and the pirates also searched for clothes, silver, and other items inside the boat. Any relatively intact clothing was stripped away.

Fisherman Slashed. After the robbery, as the pirates were about to leave, one of the boatmen attempted to seize a weapon from one of the bandits. Another pirate, wielding a sharp axe, suddenly slashed the boatman's face three times. The boatman, covered in blood and in extreme pain, fell to the ground. The pirates then jumped onto their boat, fully plundered, and fled.

Unable to Reach Shanghai. After being robbed, the fishing boat was unable to continue to Shanghai. The fish inside the boat had been completely looted, and the boatman was injured. Therefore, they had to go to Ningbo from Dinghai nearby, sending the severely injured boatman to the hospital for treatment. Meanwhile, someone was sent to Shanghai to report to the local fishing industry authorities, requesting the arrest of the pirates and protection of fishing boats. This incident occurred on the night of the 24th.

Second Academic Lecture of the Municipal Dentists Association

Dr. Xu Shaoming, Doctor of Dental Surgery, Lectures on Common Knowledge of Tooth Extraction Anesthesia

The Municipal Dentists Association held its second academic lecture at 6 PM last night in the auditorium of the new clubhouse of the Xuanyuan Temple in Xiaopilong Lane, Chenghuang Temple. Dr. Xu Shaoming, Doctor of Dental Surgery from the United States, was invited to the meeting to give a lecture. More than 160 members attended. First, Chairman Chen Runsheng reported and gave an introduction, and then Dr. Xu took the stage to give a lecture on common knowledge of tooth extraction anesthesia. He first discussed disinfection methods (explaining instrument disinfection, syringe disinfection, and surgical site disinfection), then anesthesia methods (general anesthesia, freezing anesthesia, and local anesthesia), and finally tooth extraction methods (explaining indications and contraindications). During his lecture, Dr. Xu distributed handouts and used instruments and diagrams to explain the key points to be noted in various aspects of tooth extraction disinfection and anesthesia, clarifying and guiding everything in detail. After Dr. Xu's lecture, Executive Director Chen Runsheng lectured on the evolution of tooth extraction techniques in China and reported on recent association work. The meeting adjourned at around 9 PM.

Sports News

Consecutive Long Shots Skillfully Hit the Basket, Lianghua Overcomes the Pirates With Great Joy, Fifty to Forty-Three, Lianghua Fights With Only Four Players in the End, Situation Extremely Tense, Lianghua Has Five Players Fouled Out, The Two Teams Will Meet Again Tonight at Shen Garden

The undefeated Pirates were finally defeated by Lianghua yesterday. Lianghua's victory was due to their outstanding fighting spirit on the one hand and the favor of luck on the other. The beautiful long shots were amazing and received endless praise. The tension of the overall situation was unprecedented in basketball games, and the enthusiasm of the crowd was even rarer. The outcome could not be predicted beforehand, and could not be judged during the competition. It was impossible to determine who would win or lose until the end of the game. The warriors of the two teams could not take their temporary advantage as the final victory. However, Lianghua finally defeated its previous opponent, the undefeated Pirates team, by a score of fifty to forty-three.

Three Players Absent

The tension and excitement of the situation can only be deeply remembered by the spectators on the scene, and cannot be fully expressed. It is impossible to convey the process of the game in writing. We can only describe it lightly here and let the readers experience the situation at that time. Lianghua's victory was a great relief for the Shanghai basketball community, and it also avenged the failure of last year. Because Lianghua's Tang Baokun was unable to arrive due to the interruption of the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) train, and Liu Zhenyuan also rested due to a hand injury, suddenly losing two main players. In the beginning, many spectators shouted the names of the two and said that it was not worth coming to see the game without Tang Baokun. In addition, the main defender Yin Hongxiang was also absent.

Long Shots Win

Fortunately, Tang and Liu did not play, otherwise Lianghua would still be defeated by the Pirates. Liu and Tang cannot make long shots. In last night's battle, it was impossible to win without long shots. Xu Zhaoxiong was a star for Lianghua. Whenever the Pirates seemed to have a chance to rise, Xu Zhaoxiong would give them a blow to the head with a long shot, thwarting their momentum. Yin Huanwen also tried his best to defend and often made long shots to contribute. Li Zhenzhong has his own special skills, which are impeccable. In short, yesterday's victory was not achieved by the strength of one or two people. The whole team had great achievements. The five official starters were sent off by four after entering, leaving only Li Zhenzhong alone. In the end, they struggled with only four people, almost causing the entire team to collapse and fail at the last minute. Zhang Jing was sent off five minutes after entering the game. The Western referee seemed to be paying special attention to him, which does not seem very clever.

The Pirates Panic

Due to the excessive tension of the situation, both sides often rushed their throws. The Pirates, who were known for their reliable free throws, only made twelve out of the opponent's twenty-seven fouls. Shi Guiya's attitude was not civilized, and his actions were mostly filled with smoke and fire. Shi Guiya contributed to Zhang Jing's early ejection. However, Shi Guiya was not sent off until the end of the game, which was somewhat unjust. Carlson's courage and calmness made him the most outstanding player on the Pirates team. His efforts made the whole team energetic. Long-legged Rhine was the most effective under the basket, whether on offense or defense, but sometimes he was clumsy and not very useful. His skills were not very good, and he could only use his tall body.

Spectacle of the Crowd

The audience was like crazy drunkards. When the game was tense, every spectator had their own expression, which cannot be described in words. After the game, their voices must have been greatly reduced. Around 5 PM, the crowd surrounded the front and back doors of the Western Youth Association. By 7 PM, the stadium was packed with no space to move. Adventurers were still walking on the one-inch-wide footholds on the railing, squeezing into the crowd. If they were a little restless, they would be in danger of falling from the upper floor. The shouts of the crowd were so loud that unless one was deaf, one would become temporarily deaf. Before the start of the game, the temporary staff of the Western Youth Association lost sight of the big picture, squeezing out the spectators outside the door who were trying to break in. The number of people who could not enter was at least twice the number of people inside. The staff of the Western Youth Association, without badges or important business, could only taste the closed door. This move was very smart and worth writing about.

Only One Point Difference

The score in the first half was twenty-one to twenty-one, with the Pirates' Smith taking the lead with the last goal. Zhang Jing was sent off at eight to five. Zhang's foul was partly intentional, and his intention was indeed promoted by Shi Guiya. Li Zhenzhong stole a cold meal, thanks to Zhang Jing's long pass, opening the record. Carlson made it three to two to take the lead. Shen Yu Gong jumped up and turned around, throwing the ball over his shoulder and hitting the target. After Shi Guiya made it five to four to take the lead again, it became Lianghua's world. Carlson and Smith's efforts made it eight to eight, but the Pirates still failed to surpass. After ten to ten, Lianghua took the lead by three or four points, or only won by one point. Later, it was twenty-one to sixteen, becoming the largest difference. With a giant two shots, Smith succeeded in a long shot in the middle of the field, thus surpassing by one point. This was the result of the first half.

Time of Triumph

The situation in the second half was very chaotic and the most tense. The Pirates made waves, showing off their power with twenty-six to twenty-one. Li Zhenzhong struggled desperately, and Yin Huanwen and Wang Shifu frequently used long shots, which were indeed successful. At twenty-nine to twenty-six, Lianghua once again took the advantage. From then on, Lianghua's brilliance was fully revealed, and their arrogance was extreme. The audience's emotions increased accordingly. Xu Zhaoxiong was quick-handed and quick-eyed, shooting as soon as he got the ball. The long distance was always successful, making it forty to thirty-one, which was the most glorious moment, and the audience was the most proud. The Pirates woke up from a dream and used long-legged Rhine to approach step by step. The score gradually narrowed, but Lianghua did not give in, and Wang Youcai and Yin Huanwen still shot accurately, still leading by forty-eight to forty.

Four Players Fight

At this time, Wang Shifu, Yin Huanwen, and Shen Yu Gong were all sent off one after another. Shi Guiya was also exempted from the battle at this time. When it was forty-eight to forty-two, Xu Zhaoxiong suddenly committed his fourth foul. After that, Lianghua could only cope with four people. The Pirates took the opportunity to rob and became even more rampant. The situation was extremely dangerous. The shouting and roaring became more intense. Li Zhenzhong finally scored a goal, and the final whistle sounded as the ball entered the basket. Lianghua's joy at this time and the frenzy of excitement it gave to the crowd would have made George Bernard Shaw beside himself with delight, unable to be humorous anymore.

Fight Again Tonight

At 7 PM tonight, the two teams must meet again at the Shen Garden basketball room. The venue is spacious, and both sides can give full play to their power. The Pirates lost on this field last night, and they will definitely retaliate with all their strength tonight. Lianghua has already won and naturally wants to maintain its victory. Since the two teams have their own private intentions, the competition will definitely be even more intense than yesterday. The referees are Brandt and Qu Hongren, and tickets are five jiao.

Zhejiang University Engineering College Shanghai Alumni Express Their Opinion on President Guo's Resignation

The Shanghai branch of the Zhejiang University Engineering College Alumni Association issued a telegram stating: "To all national organizations, legal entities, newspapers, schools, and the people of the nation, Zhejiang University has always valued integrity. However, since Guo Renyuan took office as president, there have been repeated disturbances. Mr. Guo has repeatedly resigned and been reinstated. It is said that this time he again used the name of preventing patriotic movements and arresting students, leading to the movement to oust Guo. There should be a public discussion about the rights and wrongs. However, the alumni of the alma mater can maintain order and attend classes peacefully in a difficult environment, taking into account both personal, school, and national interests. Our association is deeply admired. Now that Mr. Guo has submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Education, our association has unlimited sympathy for the alma mater. In addition to telegraphed to the Ministry of Education to approve his resignation, we also hope that people from all walks of life will uphold the principle of safeguarding education and provide rational assistance. We are deeply grateful to the public." Sincerely, Shanghai Branch of the Zhejiang University Engineering College Alumni Association, December 21st.

Distressed by the Crisis of National Affairs: Huang Bianqun Commits Suicide in Germany

Studying Engineering Machinery in Germany with Determination and Perseverance - Severely Stimulated by the Situation in North China -

(New Cooperative News Agency, Berlin) Huang Bianqun, a Chinese engineering student from Kaiping, Guangdong, studying in Berlin, Germany, learned of the seriousness of the situation in North China on the evening of November 22nd. He was greatly angered and, in a moment of excessive stimulation, committed suicide in his Berlin residence. After this incident occurred, the Chinese Embassy in Berlin immediately telegraphed back to China, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a telegram to inquire in detail. The reply confirmed the incident. He left behind 2,400 marks in tuition fees. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has notified his family to handle the aftermath. Mr. Huang was sent to the United States to study at public expense by Tsinghua University in 1927. In 1929, he obtained a Bachelor of Electrical Engineering degree from Purdue University. In 1930, he obtained a Bachelor of Mechanical Engineering degree. He then went to MIT, where he obtained a Master of Electrical Engineering degree in 1931 and a Master of Mechanical Engineering degree in 1932. He interned in factories and then went to Europe for further study. In 1933, he obtained a degree in Mechanical Engineering from the Berlin Institute of Technology in Germany. After that, he began working on his doctoral dissertation. Because he was concerned about the development of highway transportation and the lack of domestic oil production in China, he focused on the problem of charcoal-powered cars, which he expected to complete next summer. Mr. Huang was determined and persevering in his studies, so when Tsinghua University telegraphed to invite him to return to China to teach, he declined. This time, he committed suicide, and our country has lost another engineering talent.

Wartime Education Work Plan (3)

Colleagues from the Education Research Institute of Zhongshan University

D. Implementation Steps

1. Submit the wartime work plans for educational administration and schools at all levels to the Ministry of Education for revision, promulgation, and implementation.

2. The Provincial Department of Education and National Universities convene meetings of principals of middle and upper schools and directors of civil education centers in the provincial capital to discuss and prepare for wartime work.

3. The director of the Provincial Department of Education and the president of the National University appoint members of the Provincial Educational Wartime Work Committee from among the university presidents, professors, county and city education bureau chiefs, middle school principals, and provincial civil education center directors in the province.

4. Members of the Provincial Wartime Work Committee are sworn into office.

5. The Provincial Wartime Work Committee hires directors of various departments.

6. The county (city) education bureau (or section) convenes meetings of principals of primary and secondary schools, directors of civil education centers, and principals of public schools in the county to prepare for wartime work.

7. The director (or section chief) of the county/city education bureau appoints members of the County Education Wartime Work Committee from middle school principals, middle school teachers, primary school principals, civil education center directors, and public school principals in the county (city).

8. Members of the County Wartime Work Committee are sworn into office.

9. The County Wartime Work Committee hires directors of various departments.

10. Each school organizes a wartime work committee.

11. Start personnel registration, needs investigation, skills training, curriculum guidance, and social work.

E. Wartime Work Plan for Universities

A. Organizational System

1. Wartime universities should be transformed into factories and military camps to cultivate leaders for various wartime tasks.

2. To achieve a moderate number of people, similar aspirations, and mutual recognition between teachers and students, wartime work in universities should be organized by college.

3. The highest authority of the university's wartime work organization is the University Wartime Work Committee, with college branches as the central organization and work groups as the basic organization.

4. It can be divided according to the nature of the work, such as poison gas defense teams, security teams, etc. Each team has 15 people and is not limited by grade level. If there are several teams for one type of work, they are called "the Xth (such as poison gas) team." There are joint team meetings to coordinate work.

5. Students should join a team in their college according to their abilities and aspirations. Each team elects one representative.

6. Professors serve as natural advisors to two teams.

7. Staff and workers are free to participate in the work of a certain team.

8. The University Wartime Work Committee has five departments: Personnel Registration, Needs Investigation, Technical Training, Curriculum Guidance, and Social Work.

9. Each team is both a constituent part of the college branch and is still governed by the corresponding part of the University Committee to ensure the consistency of work throughout the school.

10. The organizational chart for each level is as follows:

B. Work Outline

1. Distribute survey forms to investigate each person's abilities and interests.

2. Classify and register various personnel.

3. Dispatch students to designated areas to investigate the needs in various aspects during wartime.

4. Change the curriculum. During wartime, set aside one-fourth to one-half of the time each week to do wartime assignments.

5. When formulating wartime work in universities, special attention should be paid to high-level technical training and mass production.

6. Assign each student to study the following new wartime teaching materials on their own:

Military Knowledge, First Aid Knowledge, Defense Knowledge, Firefighting Knowledge, Traffic Management Knowledge, Crowd Command Methods, Food Management Knowledge, Military Geography, Current Affairs Discussion.

7. Invite professors to participate in the work and assess students' self-study achievements in new wartime teaching materials at any time.

8. Announce wartime news at any time.

9. Members of each college divide into teams according to their strengths to take on a kind of work. Examples are as follows:

10. College of Liberal Arts - Domestic and foreign propaganda, military training for male students, first aid training for female students, teaching the public.

11. College of Law - Formulate diplomatic plans based on international law, maintain public order, stabilize the whole military training for male students, first aid training for female students

12. College of Science - Manufacture poison gas, manufacture gas masks, manufacture fire extinguishers, survey the terrain.

13. College of Engineering - Survey the terrain, repair railways, manufacture military supplies, dig underground kilns to make fire extinguishers, repair public places, install telegraphs and telephones.

14. College of Medicine - Manufacture medicines, compile first aid guides, study new tactics, provide nursing, and serve in war zone hospitals.

15. College of Agriculture - Distribute seeds, manufacture fertilizers, compile planting guides, manufacture food, provide fuel.

16. If it is an independent college, or a university with only three colleges, it may refer to and concurrently do the work of other colleges.

17. Universities should have various equipment to meet wartime needs.

18. The funds needed for wartime work, in addition to being supplied by the government, are also freely donated by members of the faculty and staff.

C. Implementation Steps

1. The president convenes an emergency wartime meeting to discuss preparations for wartime work. 2. Members of the University Wartime Work Committee are sworn in. 3. Members of the College Branch Committee are sworn in. 4. Each college distributes ability and interest survey forms, which are filled out by all faculty, staff, and workers of the university. 5. Each college tallies the survey results and announces the names of the members of each team in the college. 6. Each team elects one representative. 7. The school committee investigates wartime needs and notifies each college to be responsible for supplementing them separately. 8. Hold a joint team meeting to formulate a work progress outline. 9. Plan funding and purchase equipment. 10. Implement training. (To be continued)

Children's Education Novel

Little Boy (1)(3)(7)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

But nothing could compensate for the loss of freedom; hours of confinement made Nanen know how precious freedom was.

In the last quiet time, when the children went to the creek to see Emmie's new boat launched, she leaned against the window, and then she had endless thoughts, hovering in her little mind. This boat has been named Shu, as a tribute to Mrs. Pei, and was originally scheduled to be launched by Nanen, she had long thought about how to break a small bottle of gallon wine on the boat's mast when the boat was launched. Now she has lost that chance, and where is Little Mei doing it? Thinking of this is due to her own mistakes, tears have welled up in her eyes; just then, a fat bee was rolling around in the yellow flower heart of a rose under the window, and she said loudly to him:

"If you have run away, go home immediately and tell your mother that you have regretted it and will never do it again."

"I'm glad to hear you give him such good advice, I think he has accepted it," Mrs. Shu said with a smile, at which time the bee had vibrated his pollen-stained wings and flew away.

A few tears have sparkled on the window sill, Nanen hurriedly wiped it away, Mrs. Shu has seen it, picked her up, placed her on her lap, and said gently.

"Do you think my mother's method of treating runaways is good?"

"Teacher, yes," Nanen replied, a day of silence was enough to subdue her.

"I hope I won't have to try again."

"I guess I won't; " Nanen said, looking up, the sincerity on her little face pleased Mrs. Shu, and she didn't say another word, because she would rather let that punishment carry out its effect, rather than diminish the effect by saying too much on the tongue.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Qiu Lang)

"It's hard to be a person," "It's hard to be a person," "It's hard to be a difficult person," no matter how you toss and turn, it always says that it's not easy to be a person! Indeed, being a person is complicated, you have to take care of everything, and you have to pay attention everywhere. In today's world where customs are not ancient and people's hearts are declining, it can be said that it is difficult to be difficult!

For example, if you have property, thieves are always coveting you, making you uneasy and unable to rest. If you don't have money, not only will others despise you, but it will also be difficult to maintain your life!

As for being smarter about spending money, others will say he is "scraping skin," and if he spends lavishly, others will blink at him "abuse." If he is too loyal to his friends, he may be deceived by others. If he is always slick, others will say he is "floating and insubstantial." If he treats his subordinates leniently, he will not be feared, and if he treats them tightly, he will be resented. If he is close to his superiors, he will be close to flattery, and if he is alienated, he will be afraid of losing favor. Therefore, it is difficult everywhere, up, down, left, and right. Only by being fair and cautious, and adopting the doctrine of the mean, can he serve as a compass for dealing with the world.

Gold and Beauty

— Rong Yu

My friend, Mr. Someone, has two statues of different styles and incompatible on his desk, which makes people laugh. One is a statue of the God of Wealth with angry eyes, a horizontal whip across his tiger, and a body covered in gold. It is obvious at a glance that it is an 18th-century Huishan product. There is also a nude statue carved out of marble, with cloudy hair and high clusters, starry eyes looking askance, bulging breasts and buttocks, and jade body completely presented. This is a Western product that is in line with the times. Putting these two things of different times and different natures together is especially striking and surprising. One day, I honestly and unceremoniously advised him to remove the God of Wealth and let the nude woman stand alone and be more energetic. He smiled and dropped two lines of scripture and said, "Fish, I want it, and bear's paw, I want it too." I didn't understand, so I asked further, "Don't you even want to throw away this worthless clay puppet and let it make a fool of itself here?" At this time, he said to me with a serious face: This clay puppet is indeed worthless. I turned it around from the mud man's burden with two corners, but what does it symbolize? Doesn't it represent the money that everyone likes? People with money love money, and people without money are also thirsting for money. Everyone in the world worships at the feet of the God of Wealth, let alone me, a mortal! So I offer it on my desk, no less than morning and evening worship, hoping that he will bless me early! After listening to his words, I retorted, "Since you worship the God of Wealth, why put a nude statue next to it to blaspheme the gods and Buddhas?" He smiled and said, "This is also the god of love I worship, what is blasphemy! From ancient times, gold and female beauty have been linked together. When a person is poor, he feels that an old woman with a yellow face is also cute. It is not right with gold. Only a stunning beauty can shine with her gold. Don't you see that every rich man is holding a modern wife! Therefore, in addition to worshiping the God of Wealth, I am still praying to the God of Love, hoping that the two of them will come down together!"

After listening to his seemingly solemn and humorous words, I was speechless to refute them; after thinking about it, I felt that there was a great truth in it, so I wrote it out for people to criticize.

Bamboo Leaf Workshop

— Zhou Zixin

The neighbors I live with are a husband and wife, and three children, a family of five. They don't have their ancestors' inheritance to sit back and enjoy the good life, nor do they have a fixed income to provide for their daily life; the whole family thrives on the small-scale bamboo leaf workshop to maintain their life, clothing, food, and shelter; everything...

Two New Toys

—

Bamboo leaf workshops are rare in the city. The scope is very narrow. Most of them are in the house where they live, leaving a piece of land to be used as a workshop. It is a manual labor life. The name is so rude, so most people who are familiar with it may have a contemptuous heart, because it is a manual labor life, a labor life.

In the morning, in the cold wind, you can hear the noisy rustling sound; lying on the window sill, you can see, sitting in the high and fluffy bamboo leaf pile, are people who are sorting out bamboo leaves, men, women, old, young;... They are busy sorting out the scattered bamboo leaves, in order to seek a reward of two copper coins per catty. The reward is so meager, so subtle, but, in this moment of morning light, they are toiling to earn a reward, which is more precious than anything else.

Sizing the work is the second step of the procedure, which can be said to be completely the life of women, the reward is much better than the sorters, but that work is not as easy as the previous one, sizing the pieces of bamboo leaves into long and wide bamboo slices, with two pieces across the open, two feet long; the calculation of the reward is also estimated by weight—catty—each catty is one point and six cents, if you are serious every day, you can also get a price of more than four corners!

"The world has changed, everything has changed! Isn't it? Just take the bamboo leaf workshop, for example. In the past, every burden sold for seven yuan, and there was a profit of two or three yuan. The business was still booming. Now it's not a way out. Every burden sells for five yuan. No one wants it in the east, and no one needs it in the west. It's still so deserted; really, the world has really changed," Lao Guan murmured to everyone he met.

Little Western Paradise

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 22: Heroic Words Move Painted Lips, Beautiful Women Gather to Discuss; False Affection Startles Jade Wrists, Poor Woman Escapes Captivity

Mrs. Liu was so modern, beckoning to him with a snow-white arm, how could he not be moved? Moreover, her attitude had softened, and she wanted to talk things over, how could he not go? So he walked in with a smile and said, "What's that? I don't need to hide." Then he walked into the room, put his hands on his hips, sat on the edge of the bed, crossed his legs, and stared at everyone. Mrs. Liu, however, folded her jade arms in her bosom and looked back at him. Jia Duocai said, "Now I'm in, what do you all have to say? I'm all ears here. Anyway, I haven't committed any crimes." Mrs. Liu stretched out her white hand, pointed at him, and said, "You lock women in the house, depriving them of their freedom, and you still say you're not guilty?" Jia Duocai said, "She's my wife, if I don't lock her in the house, should I put her on the street?" He was also extremely angry, and saying the words "small wife" was a great taboo. All the ladies were enraged and pointed at him. One said, "This man's words are such an insult to women, we must teach him a lesson!" With just this one sentence, everyone began to clamor. Some leaned forward a little, pointing their arms straight at Jia Duocai's face. He thought to himself, if they slap me, who am I going to settle the score with? So he turned and ran outside, jumping around in the hallway and saying, "You only care about other people's business, but you don't care about yourselves. You talk about women's liberation, but first liberate yourselves. Why do you put rouge on your faces, perm your hair, wear high heels, and act like playthings?" As soon as he said this, something bright and dazzling, carrying auspicious air, rushed towards his head. Looking back, he felt something whip him. At the same time, he heard a clatter, and a teapot full of water flew past his head and shattered on the ground. Jia Duocai thought to himself, even if I said something wrong, why treat me with such harsh methods? Before this question could be answered, another dark object hit him in the chest—a leather shoe. From there, many things rained down on him. At this time, even if Jia Duocai had a hundred mouths, he couldn't say a word. He just stretched his hands into the air and waved them wildly. Bei Hai only wanted to watch the fun and was very calm, just spreading a newspaper in front of him, resting his hands on the table and watching. He peeked at Jia Duocai burrowing forward, burrowing into Little Western Paradise. The ladies stood in the hallway, gesticulating and clamoring. (384)

A Little Chat on Novels

Old Novels

— Tian Hen

It is also an incomprehensible thing that old novels have suddenly become popular in this modern era a month ago. The "Romance of the Three Kingdoms" and "Water Margin," which have latent influence in society, need not be mentioned! Even those less commonly seen old novels are very popular. There are old novel stalls everywhere, and the people setting up these stalls may not have been selling books before. Since they specialize in old novels, it is naturally because there are many buyers that they specialize in selling them. Furthermore, seeing that the number of these book stalls is increasing, it is evident that the sellers must be able to make a living from it. Therefore, one can imagine how popular old novels are at the moment.

Some people think that old novels are popular because they are cheap. However, this is not entirely the case. At most, it is only one of the reasons. This can be proven by looking at the cheap new novels in bookstores, which do not sell as well as old novels. The biggest reason is probably that old novels are more interesting and readable, and they happen to be cheap and easy to buy, which creates this temporary phenomenon of popularity.

We believe that although the content of old novels no longer conforms to modern trends, it would be extreme to say that reading them is completely useless. At the very least, apart from some descriptions involving superstition, old novels are quite capable of fully developing China's inherent virtues, and their influence on readers is still positive. It is a pity that the old novels sold at the book stalls now have too many errors and inconsistencies in their writing, and the proofreading is too careless! Compared to the old novels published by the World Book Company, there is no problem of careless proofreading. However, it is a pity that they have not published many so far. In addition to the first batch of ten titles, including "Dream of the Red Chamber," the most recent publications only include more than ten titles, such as "Golden Lotus" and "Romance of the States." Besides being meticulously proofread and beautifully bound, they also highlight the special features of each title and include textual research, re-evaluating the value of old novels, which can be considered an important work that adapts to the environment!

Amusements

The Drama Club of Students Studying in Japan

— Ji Yun

The drama, which has been declining in our country for a long time, is unexpectedly budding vigorously among students studying in Japan. This is thanks to several compatriots studying literature and art, holding the determination to revive drama with art. This time, they established the "Chinese Drama Troupe" for the first time in Japan, using the Tsukiji Little Theater for their maiden performance. The results were very good, giving the Japanese and fellow students a good impression. The plays for the second and third performances have also been announced. There is a great momentum for outstanding achievements and efforts, creating new activities for students studying in Japan.

Having not seen the drama of the motherland for a long time, I was of course eager to experience the flavor of the motherland upon hearing the news of the "Chinese Drama Troupe's" performance. Therefore, the performances were held for two consecutive days, two performances each day, and they were all full. In the theater, everything was handled by the students studying in Japan, except that the seating arrangements were made by Japanese women. The audience were of course all compatriots, greeting each other very warmly. Several people brought their Japanese girlfriends to watch Chinese dramas they had never seen before. Several Japanese police officers were sitting in the last few rows, staring blankly. I'm afraid there were no Japanese who came to study Chinese drama seriously.

There were two plays in total. One was "Breaching the Dike" by Wu Tianjun, which resembled a fragment from the famous novel "The Earth." It depicted a village in the Yangtze River basin this year, where Old Man Wang's son was arrested for offending the landlord Master He (the drama begins after the arrest). The eldest son, Jin Gui, also had a falling out with Mr. Wu, who was collecting donations for dike construction. So Mr. Wu instigated Master He to capture Jin Gui again, forcing him to repair the dike. Jin Gui felt it was his duty to repair the dike, so he left his old father and wife. However, it was too late, and the dike collapsed. Mr. Wu took the opportunity to push Jin Gui into the water. After hearing the news, his wife also jumped into the water to follow her husband in death, leaving only Old Man Wang and his young daughter, Xiao Mao. Initially, because they were reluctant to part with their property, they refused to escape. As a result, the water had already flooded the house, and they could not leave. They begged Master He and Mr. Wu for help with their ferry, but they were refused. They had no choice but to hold each other and wait for death. Chen Cejun's Jin Gui, Li Yuexuan's Xiao Mao, Shi Tian's Old Man Wang, and Mary's wife all performed very well. When they were in pain and screaming wildly, they all shed tears like rain. The reporter also grew up in a watery village in the Yangtze River basin, and this kind of thing was almost personally experienced. I remember during the floods, watching my kind father look at the sky with a worried face, my heart ached even more. Therefore, from the opening to the closing, the tears of sympathy never stopped, which shows that their performance was very real.

The second play was "The Inspection Commissioner," which was adapted from the original Russian play by Gogol into a Chinese drama. It depicted a wandering young man who was stuck in a hotel and mistaken by local officials as a secret inspection commissioner. He received a grand welcome and hospitality, and the county magistrate, judge, and school principal all offered bribes and flattery. Later, he moved into the county magistrate's house and had romantic affairs with the county magistrate's wife and daughter. As a result, he had to escape, and the matter was exposed. At that time, the real inspection commissioner finally arrived. This was a satirical comedy that vividly portrayed the corruption of the officialdom. However, because the original play was set in Russia, many places, such as kneeling on the ground to propose marriage, the county magistrate bringing out his wife and daughter to entertain, and moving the commissioner into the house, were not common in China. However, the performance was very lively, but because the structure was loose, it was not as intense as "Breaching the Dike."

Before each act, there was a sound of a gong, I don't know what it meant. If it were replaced with Chinese and Western music, it would be more pleasant to listen to. Or adding a few sections of music to complement the performance, it might be more colorful. The scenery was simple but did not contradict the plot. The use of electric lights to represent thunder, rain, and sunlight was meaningful. The troupe leader spent one or two months of hard work, making this maiden performance very admirable to the audience, which was not easy.

Using a Kilowatt-Hour Meter to Measure Resistors

— Pao

A kilowatt-hour meter, also known as a Kilo-watt hour meter, is used by power plants to measure the amount of electricity used by customers. Most people who have electric lights installed have one. With a kilowatt-hour meter, we can indirectly measure the resistance of a resistor in ohms.

When measuring, first turn off all the lights and all electrical appliances. Connect the two ends of the resistor to be measured to the wires, and record the amount of electricity used in a certain period of time. Then use the following formula (using the second formula) to calculate the resistance of the resistor in ohms.

In the formula, V is the voltage in volts, A is the current in amperes, T is the time in hours, and W is the electricity used in kilowatt-hours.

Now, for clarity, let's use the results of an experiment as an example, as follows:

A resistor (known to be 2000 ohms) was measured in Shanghai using the above method. The voltage V was 220 volts. In one and a half minutes, the disc of the kilowatt-hour meter rotated three times. The kilowatt-hour meter stated that the disc rotated 4800 times per kilowatt-hour. Therefore, we know that W is 3/4800 kilowatt-hours, and T is 1.5/60 hours. V is 220 volts. Substituting these values into the second formula above, we can calculate R as in the third formula.

The answer R is 1936 ohms, which differs from the 2000 ohms stated on the resistor by only 3.2%.

When measuring with this method, one should pay attention to whether the resistor being measured is heating up. If it is heating up significantly, the current should be turned off immediately, otherwise an accident may occur.

A Powerful Three-Tube Radio for Home and Travel

— Xue Lun

Our purpose in assembling a radio ourselves is always to be economical, durable, and efficient. However, it is really not easy to have all three. The problem of electricity is the most difficult to solve, because we young amateur enthusiasts are definitely not staying in one place. If we assemble the radio as an AC-powered one, and we have to take it to a place without a power plant for livelihood reasons in the future, then this radio will be almost useless. If you are currently living in a remote rural area, there is definitely no city electricity, so you must choose vacuum tubes such as the 30 type when assembling the radio. However, once you have something to do and have to live in the city, you still have to change the batteries often, wouldn't that be a great injustice?

I think fellow enthusiasts often encounter this kind of problem. Well, I am also one of the sufferers. As the saying goes, "Learn a lesson from a loss, right?" Last month, my AC radio vacuum tube broke, so I decided to switch to a 9.3v car tube. Fortunately, it is very easy to rewind the secondary coil of the power transformer. It took me a day to assemble a home and travel radio. A few days ago, I took it to play on Ma Ji Mountain. A High-Performance Two-Tube Broadcast Radio

— Qi

A good radio relies entirely on perfect design and precise manufacturing. This is a universally recognized iron rule. Looking back at the inferior radios that are flooding the market today, their design is outdated and their installation is extremely sloppy. Not to mention the parts used, which are all of extremely poor quality. Just imagine, is it not ridiculous to seek so-called "excellent performance" on this kind of radio? But in fact, there are puzzling things, that is, many short-sighted people, because of greed for temporary cheapness, (?) spare no effort to disregard national interests and buy those inferior machines that are almost waste. When a hundred kinds of problems arise afterwards, making it unbearable to clean up, then it is useless to call out that they have been fooled, but it is already of no help to the matter. This kind of fool can be fooled is not worthy of pity, but the country has suffered a loss invisibly!

Everyone does not want to be fooled after paying money, right? Then let me introduce to you an easy-to-make two-tube radio, which guarantees that you can get satisfactory results from it.

This machine uses two new types of vacuum tubes. One is 6F7, using its pentode part for radio frequency amplification, and the triode part for regenerative grid-leak detection. The other is 79, used for two-stage resistance-coupled audio frequency amplification. Therefore, both selectivity and volume are quite satisfactory. The tone quality is particularly soft because 79 is used for resistance-coupled low amplification. Compared with using 42 and other powerful amplification tubes, it is naturally much better.

Speaking of the installation of this machine, there is not much difficulty. The key is the adjustment of the two high-frequency coils. In fact, if you pay a little attention when winding the coil, and the coaxial capacitors used are of good quality, there is nothing to worry about. The whole machine is installed on a 22''x5''x8'' aluminum chassis. Except for large parts such as vacuum tubes, coaxial capacitors, and coil wires, the rest are placed under the chassis. The 6F7 vacuum tube and the two coils should be shielded to avoid induction.

The reason why I did not draw the power supply part of this machine is nothing more than to allow everyone to change it freely, or to use existing ones to save money. As for the power transformer I used, it was specially designed for this machine and wound by myself. The primary input line is 220v, the secondary high voltage is 250v 30M.A. Filament heating voltage is 6.3v 1.2A. The rectifier tube used is I-V, which is economical and power-saving; in addition, there is another advantage, that is, the filament voltage only needs to wind one 6.3v one. However, if you already have an existing similar powerful three-tube machine's power transformer, then you can also try to modify it for use. The coil manufacturing method and application parts are listed below to conclude.

The Effective Value of AC Voltage

— Hua Xin

Why can AC current be measured in amperes and AC voltage be measured in volts? The answer to this question can be easily solved as long as we recognize that when the heat effect produced by AC flowing through a resistor in one second is the same as the heat effect produced by one ampere of DC flowing through this resistor in one second, it is one ampere. The heat generated by 5 amperes of DC flowing through a 2-ohm resistor per second is 50 watts. The heat generated by 5 amperes of AC flowing through a 2-ohm resistor per second is also 50 watts. Such an ampere is called the effective value of AC current (Efective Value). The effective value of AC current is equal to the maximum value of the current (Maximum Value) divided by the square root of 2, in other words, it is equal to the maximum value multiplied by (0.607). Let I represent the effective value of AC, and Im represent the maximum value of AC, then

(Note: The square root of 2 is equal to 1.414). Similarly, the effective value of AC voltage is also the product of its maximum value and 0.707. Let E be the effective value of AC voltage, and Em be the maximum value of AC voltage, then

Or

In addition to the maximum value and effective value, there is also the so-called average value (Average Value), which is often used when AC is rectified into DC. The average value is the average number of instantaneous values (Instanteucoaus value) in half a cycle of AC, which is equal to the maximum value multiplied by 0.637. Let Ia be the average value of the current, and E be the average value of the voltage, then

The maximum value, effective value, and average value are often used in wireless radio transmitting and receiving lines. The voltage measured by ordinary AC voltmeters is the effective value of the voltage, and the measured current is the effective value of the current. The current measured by the DC ammeter inserted in the vacuum tube plate circuit is the average value of the plate current. The maximum value can sometimes also be measured with a vacuum tube voltmeter (Peak Vacuum-Tube Voltmofer).

Special Feature: China's Tea Industry (Part 2)

— Yi Bai

Country Quantity Percentage

Soviet Union 257,470 33.11%

United Kingdom 193,371 34.85%

United States 54,294 6.97%

India 11,782 1.51%

Turkey 4,673 0.51%

Japan 326 0.04%

South Africa 282 0.02%

Other 256,073 32.90%

Total 778,271 100.00%

The Soviet Union's 33.11% share is undoubtedly the largest market for Chinese tea consumption. In 1915, Chinese tea exports to the Soviet Union (Imperial Russia) reached a massive 1.16 million dan, accounting for over half of China's total tea exports. Later, due to the Russian Revolution and the blockade by various countries, the economy was in a state of panic, and frugality became widespread. The export of Chinese tea to that country also sharply declined, plummeting to 11,000 dan in 1920. By 1925, it gradually recovered to 200,000 dan. After 1929, due to the severance of diplomatic relations between China and Soviet Russia, it decreased again from 370,000 dan to 40,000 dan in 1930. When China and the Soviet Union announced the resumption of diplomatic relations in 1932, Chinese tea exports to the Soviet Union also recovered to 230,000 dan. Although it increased steadily from 1932 to 1934, it never regained the level of 1929. This is due to the Soviet Union's own tea cultivation and the export of Japanese Ceylon tea to the Soviet Union.

The Soviet Union's tea industry is a product of the Five-Year Plan. According to a report by the Soviet government, it has spent four years and 25 million rubles specifically on developing the tea industry. Furthermore, according to a recent announcement by the capital of the Caucasus Republic, Tbilisi, the output of green tea in 1935 is expected to reach 12 million kilograms. The tea area will increase by 16,000 hectares. Over 64,000 farmers are engaged in the tea industry, forming 830 collective farms and 15 state farms. This is one of the reasons for the decline in Chinese tea exports to the Soviet Union. In addition, the intrusion of Japanese, Indian, and Ceylon teas into the Soviet market is also a reason for the decline in Chinese tea imports to the Soviet Union.

The loss of the Soviet market is a death sentence for the Chinese tea industry. The second hope rests solely on the United Kingdom. Sixty-seven years ago, the United Kingdom was China's only market. In 1868, of the 1.54 million dan of total Chinese tea exports, the United Kingdom accounted for 1.22 million dan. From 1868 to 1888, the United Kingdom's annual consumption of Chinese tea was consistently above 1 million dan. However, after 1889, due to the sharp increase in tea production in India, the United Kingdom, which had been China's only market, was seized by India, resulting in the quantity of tea exported to the United Kingdom falling from 890,000 dan in 1889 to 240,000 dan in 1900. In the 30 years or so from 1901 to the present, the average annual amount has been around 200,000 dan. It truly evokes a feeling of unbearable regret! The recent inability of Chinese tea to operate in the United Kingdom is due to the decline in British exchange rates. Japanese tea is taking advantage of this global currency struggle and implementing a devaluation dumping policy in markets such as the United Kingdom, so Chinese tea is truly under triple pressure. The situation of Chinese tea in the American market is exactly the same as in the United Kingdom. Since 1926, Chinese tea exports to the United States have declined all the way. According to the China Daily News (Lianqiao She Batavia Report) of October 25, 1935, all tea imported by the United States in 1886 was produced in China. By 1906, Chinese tea imports to Japan were also numerous, a decision by India. Later, India and Japan engaged in tea cultivation, which has now become increasingly developed. Not only do Japan and India not need to rely on China for tea, but they are also gradually seizing China's market in the United States. Now, in addition to tea from China, Japan, and Java being imported and sold in the United States, there is also an increasing daily amount of products from Ceylon and Annam. China's overseas tea market has not only been taken away or invaded by emerging tea-producing countries, but there is also the abnormal phenomenon of tea from emerging tea-producing countries being imported into China. According to the China Daily News of October 30 this year: "Javanese tea imports into China were 595,561 kilograms in 1931, 326,524 kilograms in 1932, 15,810 kilograms in 1933, and 97,229 kilograms in 1934. In four years, the total reached 1,033,254 kilograms." Furthermore, according to the China Daily News of August 25, 1935: "From January to July 1935, foreign tea imports into China totaled over 150,000 dan, including 4,902 dan from India, 29,004 dan from Ceylon, 15,519 dan from Hong Kong, 29,937 dan from Japan, 48,747 dan from Java, and 14,097 dan from other countries, totaling 92,518 taels of customs gold, equivalent to 167,294 yuan in national currency. At the same time, it can also be seen that China's trade structure is unsound!"

The tea industry development policies of various emerging tea-producing countries are even more active during this period of global economic panic. For example, the Javanese government is implementing publicity policies to develop the Javanese tea industry. In September of this year, the amount was 7,000 shields. This huge publicity expense is compensated by levying a tax of 9.7 cents per hundred kilos of tea.

Beriberi

— Dr. Yao Erchang

This disease is caused by exclusively eating highly refined white rice. This has been proven by experimenting with feeding chickens and pigeons white rice. The symptoms include headaches, loss of appetite, nausea, insomnia, diarrhea, bloody stools, and various beriberi symptoms.

Rice contains essential vitamins A, B, and C, as well as minerals, fats, and proteins, which are essential for human health. Once refined, these elements are lost with the bran and germ, leaving very little and unable to maintain health. Therefore, people in Shanghai are often weak and sick, more so than rural residents. It is said that this is due to eating top-grade white rice, and this is indeed believable.

Commentary

"The Farce in North China"

— Meng Ruo

It is said that the North China issue has come to an end, because the Hebei-Chahar Political Council has now been declared established, which pleases a certain country. However, although there are many optimists, a portion of "ignorant" young students still hold dissenting views. However, this is also inconsequential. Anyway, the independence of five provinces has been reduced to the autonomy of two provinces, and victory still lies on this side. However, hearing foreign criticism calling this play "The Farce in North China" is a bit much. Moreover, they pointed out that the characters who took the stage this time were the ×× warlord, the × Foreign Ministry personnel who joined forces with the warlord, the characters created by the warlord, and the supporting Chinese autonomists. To call the Chinese autonomists "supporting roles" is even more sarcastic. In fact, from the stage, the Chinese autonomists originally occupied the position of the protagonist in this "farce." To say they are "supporting roles" means that foreigners either do not understand Chinese opera or intentionally insult them. Of course, if this play is a "puppet show" with someone pulling the strings behind the scenes, then we cannot know.

Fortunately, as soon as the play opened, a "jumping crown" came out to announce to the audience that in the future, all matters regarding rehearsals and actors would be based on the opinions of the audience. If the audience likes it, we will do it; if they don't like it, we will stop, and we will never deviate. From this point of view, it is fair and just. However, we feel that before this play was staged, everyone tried their best to prevent it from being performed. In particular, they expressed dissatisfaction with certain famous actors. Even though we tried our best to prevent it, and even though we were dissatisfied, the play was still performed, and it was quite lively. The so-called opinions of the audience are just grandstanding and deceitful words.

However, now that the play has been staged, whether we like it or not, we will watch it. Regardless of whether the characters on stage are grandly high-ranking or clowns making jokes, whether they are rehearsing "Losing the Street Pavilion" or "Taking Chengdu," we will, as an audience, closely monitor them from the front of the stage. If they are loyal ministers on stage, we will applaud and praise them. If they are treacherous ministers, we will scold them or simply pull them off the stage. We must not let them act arbitrarily and turn the stage upside down. But what worries me is that they will hire several strong men as bodyguards behind the stage, which will make things difficult.

In recent years, there have been many Chinese operas. After the "Manchurian Opera" was finished, this "North China Opera" was performed, which is too lively. I wonder when the gongs and drums will stop?

Winter Night Musings

— Simon

I. Rain and Snow Falling

Scattered fine snowflakes, mixed with the misty rain of dusk, the streets of November, also scattered with endless melancholy. The passing vehicles were so hurried, the footsteps of pedestrians were also hurried, and the silhouettes of the vehicles quickly disappeared into the dusk of the rain and snow-shrouded gloomy corners, but the people lagged far behind. Quickened the pace, tucked the neck into the high collar, but the road is slippery, be careful not to stumble carelessly, and then can't help but look at the vast future with melancholy, a strange anxiety in the heart, why can't I always move forward? Isn't a warm and comfortable home waiting for me to return nearby? Why does it feel more and more distant, as if wandering on a long journey with no end in sight? There is a feeling of nameless sadness. The rain and snow have already soaked the whole body, maybe they are falling harder. But you have never considered taking shelter, nor have you ever thought of hiding under the eaves of a shop for a while, except for secretly cursing in your heart, you just rush forward, you have forgotten all thoughts, leaving only one simple thought—dear home, let me grow wings under my arms and fly up immediately, suddenly you have such a miraculous fantasy.

As if thrown from one world into another, when you step on the threshold of your home, you can't help but jump in, laugh childishly, take a deep breath of the warm air, exhale the frustration that filled your chest just now, quickly change your clothes, and your whole body feels relaxed to the bone.

If you just stroll to the window, look back, at the desolate street scene under the rain and snow that sent you back, the blurred figures of the pedestrians who continue to come behind you, you use a completely different, distant emotional perspective to appreciate and savor the mood.

After all, there is a lovely home, and beautiful seasons will always be waiting for you. But huddled in the streets and alleys, under the invasion of rain and snow, it is truly the season of dreams for those who have no home to linger in. Just accompany the icy wind, watch the rain and snow falling, and send and welcome the long winter night.

II. Wine

On such ice-bound days, what makes people feel most warm is a relatively quiet house with a stove burning. If you can leisurely stay indoors all day, reading some books you like, and take a stroll when you are tired, the time will pass very easily, and besides, the winter days are very short. If possible, you would never want to step out of the door again.

And when night comes, the cold may be even heavier, drink a little wine to warm up, thinking, just then the drinking companions come to visit. So the prepared wine is brought out bottle by bottle, and simple dishes will not hinder the drinking pleasure at all, just that there should be endless wine to drink. So a few people sit by the stove, slowly sipping, warming themselves by the fire, and chatting. Watching the red tongues of fire in the stove rise fiercely, drinking, drinking passionately the red wine, even without knowing how much they have drunk, gradually their faces also turn red. The emotions you restrained cannot help but suddenly become uninhibited, because wine makes you forget yourself, and it also makes you temporarily forget your sad heart. Everyone laughs loudly, talks, and tells secret love stories, but maybe your emotions become fragile instead, you lower your head and sigh quietly, because other people's words unintentionally ignite your faded memories of love, so everyone will sigh for your sigh, but when you suddenly laugh wildly again, wine makes you so naughty. And the wine is endless, and the words are rich and endless. Everyone is intoxicated, the room is full of playful laughter and beautiful words, the heart is floating, what else is there to worry about? Even if it's so cold that your hands and feet are frozen stiff, who would think of it? It's spring in winter, you shout, abandoning everything outside yourself, don't wake up, you are willing to sink forever into this state of darkness, in the icy and lunar days, only such longing can satisfy yourself.

First Snow

— Xinye

The fierce northwest wind blew away the pale yellow sun again, and the surroundings were so cold as if immersed in the Arctic Circle. The dogs in the village had already sneaked into their houses, and the old hens hid in the woodpile, afraid to come out.

Suddenly, goose-palm-like snowflakes were also floating in the sky, flying in the air like plum petals, flying onto the roofs, trees, and ground, gradually piling up. A flock of homeless crows flew around and cawed in the sparse forest of bare branches.

"Rain and snow for three nine days, no firewood and no rice, the bitter coptis weather has arrived again. The pig feed beans at home have already been eaten up. I really don't know how to get through these three nine harsh winter days"! Sanbao's wife sat in the doorway of the stove, weaving straw sandals, looking at the smoke-like snowflakes flying in the courtyard, sighing with cold air, a heavy depression covering her expressionless face. Beside her on the ground crawled a five or six-year-old child, his body wrapped in thick, tattered cotton, wrapped as if he were a wooden pig; one of his dirty little hands, frozen like red radishes, was stuck in his mouth, constantly digging, tears and snot drawing a big painted face on his face, already separating the boundaries. In that thin outline, only a pair of glossy black eyes were active, but a wooden and large body kept crawling on the ground and rolling: "Mom, I'm hungry, Mom, I want to eat"! He cried like this.

"Sigh, eat, in this kind of year, the days of starving to death are behind us"! She dragged the child up from the ground. At this time, Sanbao stumbled in drunk from the back door, almost bumping into the child:

"Maotou, you, you're crying... again"? He squinted his flowery eyes, hummed his nose, and said incoherently, a very unpleasant smell of alcohol spraying straight onto his wife's face; so she glared at him hatefully without good temper, and scolded loudly:

"You瘟殺的, you're happy, aren't you? Where did you go to get your fill of yellow soup? The pig feed beans at home are all eaten up, I'll see how you get through these three nine cold days. Now, while the weather isn't freezing yet, you don't think of something to do, just loafing around all day long..."

Page 18

"What to do? You go think of it! You weave a few pairs of straw sandals all day long, have you ever sold them for any money!" He replied, sitting down on the threshold, his hands rubbing each other.

"What a joke, you men can't think of a way, so you want a woman to think for you, you're really not ashamed"!

"In this day and age, what's there to be ashamed or not ashamed of: the fields were washed away by the flood and nothing was harvested, jobs can't be found, anyway, starving to death is right in front of us"! He wrung the corner of his clothes hard, rested his head on the door frame, and opened a pair of lifeless eyes.

The snow in the sky was falling more and more fiercely, and the wind seemed to be stronger than just now. The old locust tree outside the door was blown howling, and the treetops were constantly curling in the air, and the magpie's nest was almost about to be thrown down by it; two magpies were standing on the ridge of Grandpa Huang's house across the street, calling incessantly.

"Sigh! Sooner or later it's all starving to death"! Sanbao suddenly thrust her head forward heavily, drooping it to her chest, and her eyelids were about to close; but her hand was picking up a rice straw core and breaking it, one section, two sections, three sections falling on the ground, lying horizontally and disorderly, just like her current state of mind. (To be continued)
