A bright moon cuts a jade axe. Plum blossoms three times, plucking a bronze pipa. Jiang Lang's dreams are filled with blossoming pens. Zhang Ziyou floats on a moon raft. Face like peach blossoms, eyebrows like the moon. The moon in the water, the flower in the mirror. May the old man under the moon transmit a mandarin duck message. May the flower slave pick up a phoenix hairpin. Worshipping the moon and burning incense, our love is sincere. Burying flowers, pitying 玉恨 knows no bounds. The guest of Xunyang with autumn moon and reed flowers. The recluse's home with lonely moon and plum blossoms. The moon palace is swept away, the phoenix tail ribbons. On the flower steps, the phoenix-headed shoes are placed. Fishing for the moon in the water, all in vain. Looking at the flowers in the mist, one's mood is naturally good. Liang Yue longs for people, sad at the moon pavilion. Wearing flowers and passing the imperial examination, walking on the streets. The goddess Su'e lives in the lunar palace. The jade girl wipes the water lily mirror. Wanting to roll up the pearl curtain to cover the night moon. Wanting to prune the bamboo and water famous flowers. Fallen flowers, crying magpies, spring sorrow water. The slanting moon and the remnant lamp, a night dream of debt. Planting flowers in the moon, guarding against rain jealousy. Leaking the moon among the flowers, relying on clouds to cover it. Drinking wine among the flowers, wandering bees dance. Playing the flute in the moon cave, attracting phoenixes to harmonize. The moon serves as a heavy quilt, the flowers as pillows. The flowers serve as four walls, the moon as a home. Heavenly flowers fall in confusion, bewitching flower shadows. The autumn moon is often round, watching the moon's splendor. Cold moon, remnant wind, lonely spring.

Yinshe Drama Troupe

Hangye (1180) From 10 PM to 10:30 PM

"Miss Youlan"

Liu Fenggang is an apprentice in Wang Delin's tailoring shop. All day long, he suffers all kinds of pain. Moreover, his false father, Zhang Sheng, often comes to threaten and beat him, causing indescribable sorrow.

One day, when the young shopkeeper was unreasonably beating him there, beating him until his head was broken and bleeding, Miss Youlan happened to come to see him. Seeing this situation, she hurriedly tried her best to comfort him, making her feel pain beyond measure. At this time, Wang Delin's nephew, Wang Huiqing, who is a university professor and also Youlan's boyfriend, passed by and saw Youlan here, feeling very strange. After greeting each other, and Youlan told him the inside story, they all helped Fenggang to go together.

Silver Jottings

— Zhi'er

The Cultural Film Company's "Parents and Children" will be screened at Jincheng starting on New Year's Day. This is a work made entirely by "new people" and deserves our special attention. (It is said that "Triumphal Song" will also be screened on New Year's Day, to be confirmed.)

At a time when the old generals are leaving or dying, the film circle is really in danger of becoming a dead city. If there are no good new people to serve as the main force, how can the old, weak, and disabled soldiers hold on?

The director of "Parents and Children", Mr. Hu Xinling, is very young. It is said that the play "Parents and Children" is also "quite" good. (Whether it is really good, let's tell the truth after watching it. Now, we can only tentatively say "quite.") And Hu Rongrong's performance as the flower girl Hu in the wedding is also "quite" good. Hopefully, these are all facts.

Yuan Meiyun and Wang Yin's "Wedding Night"

"Little Overlord" to be Screened

Another New Work by James Cagney

Since "Each One is Brave", James Cagney has starred in several films in succession, but among these many films, the most satisfying is the recent "Little Overlord" Frisco Kid (this film is scheduled to be screened at the Grand Theater on New Year's Eve). This "Little Overlord" tells the story of the 18th century, in a barbaric area of San Francisco, where there was no law, no culture, and the whole city was full of violent thugs. Murder and arson were commonplace. A sinister little overlord was born at that time. His lips were stained with women's rouge, and his fists were stained with the blood of his enemies. James Cagney, playing such a role in this film, is of course very suitable for his personality. There are many dangerous scenes in the film, and there is no slack from beginning to end. It is indeed very rare.

Several Hardships During the Production of "Triumphal Song"

The completion of a film really requires the efforts and spirit of many people, especially "Triumphal Song". It did encounter many difficulties. Now let me talk about some of the hardships during the production, which can also be considered a memorandum.

The start of "Triumphal Song" was in a cold winter years ago. Because the plot is set against a drought, we had to start with the interior scenes first. However, the weather was bitterly cold, and although the lights were strengthened, the actors were still shivering with purple lips while acting in thin clothes. Qin Tong even fell ill.

When the interior scenes were finished, it was already the hot summer. The group filmed exterior scenes in Panjiabu, Zhuji, Zhejiang for 25 days. When they returned, everyone had turned into black charcoal, and because the mosquitoes were as fierce as tigers, seven or eight people were lying in bed for more than a month before getting up.

When filming the lotus pond scene in Suzhou, it was already late autumn. Although the earth still had residual heat, the lotus pond under the shade was as cold as ice. The photographer Wu Weiyun and his assistant Wang Chunquan worked naked in the pond for a day and were attacked by the cold air when they returned.

When filming the opening of the dam, it happened that the actors had to be naked, but at this time it was the harsh winter with the north wind blowing, and the state of suffering was really beyond words.

In summary, the production of "Triumphal Song" really suffered a lot. The above is just a part of it.
